    window.googletag = window.googletag || { cmd: [] };

    googletag.cmd.push(function () {

      /* =============================
         CONFIGURAÇÕES GLOBAIS
      ============================== */

      googletag.pubads().setCentering(true);

      googletag.pubads().enableLazyLoad({
        fetchMarginPercent: 300,
        renderMarginPercent: 100,
        mobileScaling: 2.0
      });

      /* =============================
         SIZE MAPPINGS
      ============================== */

      window.__gptSizeMaps = window.__gptSizeMaps || {};

      /* ---------- TOP ---------- */
      window.__gptSizeMaps.top = googletag.sizeMapping()
        .addSize([1024, 0], [[970, 250], [970, 90], [728, 90]])
        .addSize([768, 0],  [[728, 90]])
        .addSize([0, 0],    [[320, 100], [320, 50]])
        .build();

      /* ---------- INLINE ---------- */
      window.__gptSizeMaps.inline = googletag.sizeMapping()
        .addSize([1024, 0], [
          [580, 400],
          [480, 320],
          [480, 75],
          [468, 60],
          [336, 280],
          [300, 250]
        ])
        .addSize([768, 0], [
          [480, 320],

          [468, 60],
          [336, 280],
          [300, 250]
        ])
        .addSize([0, 0], [
          [300, 250],
          [336, 280]
        ])
        .build();

      /* ---------- SIDEBAR ---------- */
      window.__gptSizeMaps.sidebar = googletag.sizeMapping()
        .addSize([1024, 0], [[300, 600], [300, 250], [160, 600]])
        .addSize([768, 0],  [[300, 250], [160, 600]])
        .addSize([0, 0],    [[300, 250]])
        .build();

      googletag.enableServices();
    });

    /* =============================
       INICIALIZAÇÃO DOS SLOTS
    ============================== */

    function __initGptSlotsOnce() {
      if (window.__GPT_SLOTS_BOUND__) return;
      window.__GPT_SLOTS_BOUND__ = true;

      googletag.cmd.push(function () {
        var slotElements = document.querySelectorAll('.gpt-slot');

        slotElements.forEach(function (el) {
          if (el.dataset.gptBound === '1') return;

          var path = el.getAttribute('data-slot');
          if (!path || !el.id) return;

          el.dataset.gptBound = '1';

          var pos = (el.getAttribute('data-pos') || 'inline').toLowerCase();
          var mapping = window.__gptSizeMaps.inline;
          var sizes = [];

          if (pos === 'top') {
            mapping = window.__gptSizeMaps.top;
            sizes = [[970, 250], [970, 90], [728, 90], [320, 100], [320, 50]];
          } else if (pos === 'sidebar') {
            mapping = window.__gptSizeMaps.sidebar;
            sizes = [[300, 600], [300, 250], [160, 600]];
          } else {
            mapping = window.__gptSizeMaps.inline;
            sizes = [
              [468, 60],
              [480, 75],
              [480, 320],
              [580, 400],
              [336, 280],
              [300, 250]
            ];
          }

          var sizesAttr = el.getAttribute('data-sizes');
          if (sizesAttr) {
            try { sizes = JSON.parse(sizesAttr); } catch (e) {}
          }

          googletag.defineSlot(path, sizes, el.id)
            .defineSizeMapping(mapping)
            .addService(googletag.pubads());

          googletag.display(el.id);
        });
      });
    }

    if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
      document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', __initGptSlotsOnce);
    } else {
      __initGptSlotsOnce();
    }
  </script>

      <script>
    (function(){
      function px(n){ return n + 'px'; }
      function bestFitFor(el, max, min, lh, lines){
        function fits(f){
          el.style.fontSize = px(f);
          el.style.maxHeight = px(f * lh * lines);
          el.style.minHeight = px(f * lh * lines);
          el.style.overflow = 'hidden';
          return el.scrollHeight <= el.clientHeight + 1;
        }
        var lo = min, hi = max, mid;
        while (hi - lo > 0.5){ mid = (hi + lo)/2; if (fits(mid)) lo = mid; else hi = mid; }
        return lo;
      }
      function fitBlock(wrap){
        var cs = getComputedStyle(wrap);
        var max = parseFloat(cs.getPropertyValue('--title-max')) || 20;
        var min = parseFloat(cs.getPropertyValue('--title-min')) || 12;
        var lh  = parseFloat(cs.getPropertyValue('--title-lh'))  || 1.25;
        var lines = parseInt(cs.getPropertyValue('--title-lines')) || 3;
        var titles = wrap.querySelectorAll('[data-fit-title]');
        if(!titles.length) return;
        var sizes = [];
        titles.forEach(function(el){
          el.style.fontSize = px(max);
          el.style.maxHeight = px(max * lh * lines);
          el.style.minHeight = px(max * lh * lines);
          sizes.push(bestFitFor(el, max, min, lh, lines));
        });
        var global = Math.min.apply(null, sizes);
        titles.forEach(function(el){
          el.style.fontSize = px(global);
          el.style.maxHeight = px(global * lh * lines);
          el.style.minHeight = px(global * lh * lines);
        });
      }
      function fitAllBlocks(){ document.querySelectorAll('[data-bnt-wrap]').forEach(fitBlock); }

      function initCarousels(){
        document.querySelectorAll('.bnt-wrap').forEach(function(wrap){
          var cont = wrap.querySelector('[data-scroll-container]');
          var nav = wrap.querySelector('.bnt-fixed-nav');
          if(!cont || !nav) return;
          cont.style.scrollBehavior = 'smooth';
          nav.querySelectorAll('.bnt-btn').forEach(function(btn){
            btn.addEventListener('click', function(e){
              e.preventDefault();
              var dir = parseInt(btn.getAttribute('data-dir')||'1',10);
              cont.scrollLeft += (dir>0?1:-1) * cont.clientWidth;
            });
          });
        });
      }

      document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function(){
        initCarousels();
        fitAllBlocks();
      });
      window.addEventListener('resize', fitAllBlocks);
    })();
    </script>

    <script>
    (function(){
        const root=document.getElementById('colunistas-e4b58286-4996-432d-9283-6a9102823f6b');
        if(!root)return;
        const viewport=root.querySelector('.colunistas-viewport');
        const track=root.querySelector('.colunistas-track');
        const prev=root.querySelector('.col-prev');
        const next=root.querySelector('.col-next');
        const dots=root.querySelector('.colunistas-dots');
        const items=[...root.querySelectorAll('.col-item')];

        function perView(){
            const w=viewport.clientWidth;
            if(w<=560) return +viewport.dataset.perMobile||1;
            if(w<=900) return +viewport.dataset.perTablet||2;
            return +viewport.dataset.perDesktop||4;
        }
        let index=0;
        function pages(){return Math.max(1,Math.ceil(items.length/perView()));}
        function setArrows(){
            const p=pages();
            prev.style.display=next.style.display=p>1?'flex':'none';
            prev.disabled=index===0; next.disabled=index>=p-1;
        }
        function go(i){
            index=Math.max(0,Math.min(i,pages()-1));
            const gap=parseFloat(getComputedStyle(root).getPropertyValue('--gap'))||28;
            const itemWidth=items[0].getBoundingClientRect().width;
            const step=index*(itemWidth+gap)*perView();
            track.style.transform=`translate3d(${-step}px,0,0)`;
            updateDots(); setArrows();
        }
        function buildDots(){
            dots.innerHTML='';
            const p=pages();
            for(let i=0;i<p;i++){
                const b=document.createElement('button');
                b.addEventListener('click',()=>go(i)); dots.appendChild(b);
            }
            updateDots(); setArrows();
        }
        function updateDots(){
            dots.querySelectorAll('button').forEach((b,i)=>b.classList.toggle('is-active',i===index));
        }

        prev.addEventListener('click',()=>go(index-1));
        next.addEventListener('click',()=>go(index+1));
        window.addEventListener('resize',()=>{track.style.transform='';index=0;buildDots();},{passive:true});

        buildDots(); go(0);
    })();
    </script>

				const lazyloadRunObserver = () => {
					const lazyloadBackgrounds = document.querySelectorAll( `.e-con.e-parent:not(.e-lazyloaded)` );
					const lazyloadBackgroundObserver = new IntersectionObserver( ( entries ) => {
						entries.forEach( ( entry ) => {
							if ( entry.isIntersecting ) {
								let lazyloadBackground = entry.target;
								if( lazyloadBackground ) {
									lazyloadBackground.classList.add( 'e-lazyloaded' );
								}
								lazyloadBackgroundObserver.unobserve( entry.target );
							}
						});
					}, { rootMargin: '200px 0px 200px 0px' } );
					lazyloadBackgrounds.forEach( ( lazyloadBackground ) => {
						lazyloadBackgroundObserver.observe( lazyloadBackground );
					} );
				};
				const events = [
					'DOMContentLoaded',
					'elementor/lazyload/observe',
				];
				events.forEach( ( event ) => {
					document.addEventListener( event, lazyloadRunObserver );
				} );

                    jQuery().ready( function () {
                        var blockUid = 'tdi_58',
                            $blockObj = jQuery('.tdi_58'),
                            modalUid = 'td-modal-newsletter',
                            $modalObj = $blockObj.find('.tdm-popup-modal-wrap'),
                            show_modal_in_composer = 'yes';

                        if( $modalObj.length && modalUid !== '' ) {
                            var tdPopupModalItem = new tdPopupModal.item(),
                                $triggerBtnObj = $blockObj.find('> .tds-button > a.tdm-btn');

                            // modal uid
                            tdPopupModalItem.uid = modalUid;
                            // block uid
                            tdPopupModalItem.blockUid = blockUid;
                            // modal object
                            tdPopupModalItem.modalObj = $modalObj;
                            // modal object
                            tdPopupModalItem.closeModals = [];
                            // modal open position
                            tdPopupModalItem._modal_open_position = 'over-screen';
                            // modal open disable site scroll
                            tdPopupModalItem._site_scroll = '1';

                            // check to see whether we are in composer or not
                                                            // we are not in composer
                                // trigger button object
                                if( $triggerBtnObj.length ) {
                                    tdPopupModalItem.triggerBtnObj = $triggerBtnObj;
                                }

                                // trigger types
                                tdPopupModalItem._modal_trigger_types = {"button":[]};

                                // modal content load
                                tdPopupModalItem._modal_content_load = '';

                                                            
                            tdPopupModal.addItem(tdPopupModalItem);
                        }
                    });
